This file is reference-only — primary CLAUDE.md is the current-state source of truth.

### J (2026-05-13 micro)

**J (2026-05-13 micro):** Four workstreams shipped same-day as G+H+I. (1) **Cover-axis fix** triggered mid-session by Josiah's aesthetic screenshot — W.U.L.D. INCORPORATED video was sitting right-of-axis within bracketed frame; root cause was `.cover-mark--video` h1 missing `margin-inline:auto` (block-level h1 with width-cap doesn't honor parent's `text-align:center` for its own box positioning); one-line fix. (2) **Library-Claude Exchange 3 response** intake from upload — LIGHT triage, all confirmations (Coda c / VAR d / why-not-suicide c), threshold for VAR material-shift flags defined (mech-diagnosis/archetype-conditional-space/MAP-DEP-positioning changes = material; prose-shape = stylistic), cadence on `session_log` per-session-close via `[WULD-FLAG: ...]` markers, relay round closed with no new forced question. (3) **Amazon book link locked** via AskUserQuestion: ASIN `B0GZ18XVTD` = "Malgré Tout: A Guide to Nothingness" (distinct from /book/'s in-development compendium). New 09th grid card shipped: `09 · Treatise / Malgré Tout / A Guide to Nothingness · Amazon · external` → `https://www.amazon.com/dp/B0GZ18XVTD` (target=_blank). Grid is now 9 actual destinations, placeholder slot gone. (4) **Footer propagation to 13 shells** via NEW `/components/footer.css`. Canonical class `.page-footer` (renamed from `.home-footer` on homepage + from `.site-footer` on templates/essay). 13-file roster: 9 page-footer shells + 1 site-footer template + 3 glossary files needing footer ADDITION. Deferred cleanup: ~160 lines of inline `.page-footer*` dead CSS still live across 8 standard shells (linked stylesheet wins on source order, dead-but-harmless); sweepable in future micro-session.

### D'' (full bundled triptych port) — 2026-05-13

**D'': full bundled triptych port shipped to `src/void-engine/index.html`** — faithful public surface of `DUAL_ENGINE_v2.html` (~374 KB pre-port / 4,390 lines; 380,265 bytes / 4,308 lines post-port after null-strip). All three engines live at `/void-engine/`: Void Engine (image-prompt builder, 222 modifiers / 15 categories), Signal Engine (992-track frequency index across 17 genres × 17 moods × 7 source playlists, link-out to YouTube Music), Transmission v2 (canvas-rendered ambient visual, 3 modes wave/particle/type cycling through 16 moods + 26 fragments). Toggle bar at top of body routes between the three (canonical `switchEngine(which)` mechanism). Six bounded transformations applied: (1) wuld.ink chrome wrap (site-header + nav, page-footer + nav.js) outside the suite's toggle bar + three engine wrappers, three header bands stack in series (site-header → #engine-toggle → per-engine .hdr); (2) Anthropic API strip per Exchange 3 B1 lock — Void Engine portion only, Signal + Transmission confirmed zero external surface per Exchange 7 D6; (3) ARCH_KEY rename to `wuld.ink:void-engine:archive`, no Signal/Transmission keys to rename per Exchange 7 D4 (both session-volatile by design); (4) wuld.ink stylesheet injection (tokens/base/nav) before canonical inline `<style>`; (5) **D5=α hash-route shim** — 22-line JS appended to toggle script block, `/void-engine/#sig` → Signal, `#trans` → Transmission, `#void` or bare → Void Engine default; (6) **D7=β Transmission canvas full-bleed under chrome** — `#trans-engine-wrap.active` becomes `position:fixed; inset:0; z-index:0`; site-header + page-footer + canonical `#engine-toggle` form opaque bands above; HUD elements offset to clear chrome bands. Engine bodies retain canonical visual register per Exchange 3 A5 (i) — Space Mono / blood-red / Courier Prime / scanline. Homepage Void card updated: `04 · Triptych` label, tag now reads "Lexicon · signal · transmission". Exchange 8 reply appended to relay doc (D1–D8 + audit-reply on suite-Claude's hash-route flag, two new flags E1 FRAGMENTS-count-delta 26-vs-25 and E2 trailing-null-padding in canonical export). Logic preservation principle held — every engine function preserved at implementation level (boot, compile, loadPreset, _runCorpusLocalMode, archGetAll/archSave, doSearch, setCat, toggleNeg, switchEngine, plus all Signal Engine catalog/decode/render functions and all Transmission canvas/MOODS/FRAGMENTS rendering functions). Only the API-mode branch was excised.

### E2 (2026-05-13 micro)

**E2 (2026-05-13 micro):** four-item arc closed via Chrome MCP — (1) audio.wuld.ink propagation re-verified (clean HTTP/2 404, no error 1014); (2) **all of sessions B + D' + D'' shipped to Cloudflare Pages this turn** — root-cause finding was that the deployed site at wuld.ink / www.wuld.ink / wuld-ink.pages.dev was still the session-A placeholder (2,783 bytes, MD5 cf33b18a) because no deploy had happened post-session-A; deploy refresh via direct-upload zip (153 KB compressed / 467 KB uncompressed / 19 files / 30 entries; built from src/ minus authoring-scaffold exclusions: fonts/README.md, templates/*, glossary/_template.html); upload via Chrome-MCP synthetic file_upload hit a known boundary limitation (NotFoundError on FileReader-read after synthetic File injection), Josiah drag-dropped manually as fallback, deploy succeeded clean (19/19 files); post-deploy verified live (apex=10,768 bytes MD5 d32227b7, /void-engine/=380,265 bytes MD5 f1841eba, 46 triptych structural markers, API-strip clean = 4 comment-residue placeholder matches only); (3) www → apex 301 redirect rule deployed via Cloudflare Rules → Redirect Rules template "Redirect from WWW to root" — wildcard pattern `https://www.*` → `https://${1}` at 301 with preserve-query-string checked; deployed despite dashboard's false-positive DNS warning (www is attached as Pages custom domain, not standalone proxied DNS, but Rules engine still inspects); verified live (www.wuld.ink/ → 301 → https://wuld.ink/; www.wuld.ink/void-engine/?test=1 → 301 → https://wuld.ink/void-engine/?test=1 with query preserved); (4) R2 custom domain audio.wuld.ink TLS minimum bumped 1.0 → 1.2 via Configure options → Minimum TLS version dropdown. **D'' live-browser smoke completed this turn:** loaded /void-engine/ in browser, Void Engine renders clean (`[wuld.ink]` site-header + VOID nav-current red underline, engine-toggle bar below, `VOID ENGINE — Sanguinolentum Vestigium` heading, 222 entries, combinatorial math `Pick-8 combinations: 128,705,283,347,445` populated, `SYSTEM ONLINE` badge, idle compiler state); clicked TRANSMISSION toggle → canvas wave-mode amber lines rendering full-viewport, site-header + toggle-bar opaque bands above, lower HUD (`MODE: WAVE · MOOD: STILLNESS · INT: 3/5` + `SIGNAL ENGINE // AMBIENT VISUAL · Illogically is.`) cleared from chrome bands — **D7=β layering confirmed working**; clicked SIGNAL ENGINE toggle → 992-track frequency index renders with italic-serif `Signal Engine // FREQUENCY INDEX` title, 17 genres + 17 mood vectors with counts (Stillness 164, Fracture 150, Melancholy 139, etc.), LIBRARY/GENERATOR toggle, search bar; tab title updates per engine switch (canonical `document.title` setter intact). Chrome-MCP synthetic-file-upload boundary documented as known limitation; future deploy refreshes via Git-deploy wire-up (when shipped) bypass this entirely.

### E3 (2026-05-13 micro, same day as E2)

**E3 (2026-05-13 micro, same day as E2):** Git-deploy wiring shipped — direct-upload pattern retired. New GitHub repo `alisendjsc-crypto/wuld-ink` (public) created and seeded with project state. Initial commit `6bc8930` amended to `0ac009a` to use the GitHub noreply email `263501734+alisendjsc-crypto@users.noreply.github.com` (satisfies GitHub's GH007 email-privacy push block). Cloudflare Pages project deleted (direct-upload only; Cloudflare doesn't allow converting direct-upload → Git-connected in-place — confirmed by inspecting every Settings + Deployments page) and recreated as Git-connected via the dedicated `/workers-and-pages/create/pages` URL. **Meaningful gotcha worth flagging for future Cowork sessions:** the unified `/workers-and-pages/create` flow ONLY creates Workers projects (with `npx wrangler deploy` deploy command), NOT Pages projects with the static-site build config Pages users actually want. The dedicated `/workers-and-pages/create/pages` URL routes to the proper 3-step Pages wizard (Select repository → Set up builds and deployments → Deploy site). Project name `wuld-ink` reused (Cloudflare reclaims same-name pages.dev hostname). Build config: framework preset None, build command empty, build output directory `src`, root directory blank, no env vars. First Git deploy from commit `0ac009a` succeeded; reclaimed `wuld-ink.pages.dev`. Custom domains wuld.ink + www.wuld.ink re-attached via Custom domains tab → Set up a custom domain; both initially showed "Verifying" + "Complete DNS setup" link; one click on "Check DNS records" each flipped both to Active with SSL enabled. ~10 min downtime in the detach-to-reattach gap (acceptable per the explicit consent gathered at session start). Sentinel empty commit `c239c9c` (`git commit --allow-empty`) pushed to main → Cloudflare webhook detected within seconds → auto-built and deployed to `4eede190.wuld-ink.pages.dev` → "Automatic deployments enabled" indicator confirmed. End-to-end git push → Pages auto-deploy wiring functional. Future deploys ship by `git push origin main` — no dashboard drag-drop ever again. **Five OneDrive/PowerShell-5.1/encoding/native-stderr issues hit during bootstrap script iteration:** (1) Cowork bash sandbox can't unlink files in OneDrive-synced workspace folder (write-once mount limitation); OneDrive sync also corrupted `.git/config` with 54 NULL bytes during sandbox-side `git init`. Pivoted to PowerShell script for user-side execution. (2) Initial PS script used here-string `@"..."@` for commit message — UTF-8 BOM stripping during Edit operations broke PS 5.1 parser. Rewrote ASCII-only with multi `-m` flag commit. (3) `$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"` combined with `2>&1` on native git commands treats stderr (e.g., `fatal: not a git repository` probes) as terminating errors; removed Stop mode + check `$LASTEXITCODE` manually. (4) GitHub blocked initial push (GH007) due to commit author using user's primary private email; resolved via `git config user.email` to noreply + `git commit --amend --reset-author --no-edit` + re-push. (5) Coordinate clicking unreliable for "Connect GitHub" tile on unified create flow; switched to `find` + ref_id clicks. **Bootstrap artifact `setup-git.ps1` shipped in the repo at root** (idempotent one-shot init+commit handling all of the above failure modes; ASCII-only, no `$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"`, `cmd /c rd /s /q` fallback for OneDrive lock cases, attribute-clearing pass before rm). Harmless if it stays — documents the bootstrap process. Removable in a future commit if desired. **Chrome MCP usage retrospective:** ~60-70 Chrome calls across E3 — repo creation (~8), Pages config (~20: includes the wasted Workers flow detour), domain detach/reattach (~15), sentinel deploy verification (~5), Cloudflare dashboard nav latency (~15). Workers vs. Pages flow detour cost ~6-8 unnecessary calls; future Pages-project create sessions should go directly to `/workers-and-pages/create/pages`. The synthetic-file-upload limitation from E2 didn't bite this session because Git-deploy bypasses file uploads entirely.

## Session-D era (Void Engine misread)

### Misread log (session D, 2026-05-13)

- **What I read:** "Void Engine — prompt tool, with Signal and Transmission components" (`docs/wuld-ink-cowork-brief.md` line 64).
- **How I parsed it:** "prompt tool" = tool that *operates on* prompts (text-in, text-out, transformation-style instrument).
- **Actual meaning:** "prompt tool" = tool that *builds* prompts (the suite's AI image-prompt builder).
- **The clarifying questions I did ask at D start were UI-shape questions** (single textarea vs. structured form, output position, registry vs. pipeline). They locked the surface details of the wrong artifact.
- **The clarifying question I did NOT ask:** *Does `/void-engine/` host an existing suite app, or is this its own new thing?* That was the architectural-origin question. Asking it would have surfaced the suite immediately and prevented the misread.
- **Failure mode to log permanently:** when a project surface shares a name with an external artifact (suite engine, library substrate, anything cross-project), ASK about origin before building. Don't infer from naming alone.

### Direction locked (rebuild fork chosen 2026-05-13)

- `wuld.ink/void-engine/` will be a faithful public **port of the suite Void Engine** (image-prompt builder, ~190 modifier entries across 12 categories, positive/negative prompt compiler, presets, chaos roll, deep scan, diagnosis modal, corpus analyzer, session archive via `localStorage`). Suite-Claude maintains the canonical source; wuld.ink-side hosts the public port.
- **Naming collision resolves cleanly under this fork:** there is ONE Void Engine. Same artifact, suite is the source-of-truth, wuld.ink is the public face.
- **Logic preservation principle for the port:** suite's JS is the canonical source. Port should preserve it as-is to the maximum extent compatible with the wuld.ink chrome. Don't re-implement what the suite has already hardened across multiple versions.
- **Styling reconciliation is the bounded transformation:** suite's CSS gets replaced with wuld.ink design tokens (`var(--c-bg)`, `var(--c-accent)`, `var(--font-mono)`, etc.); suite's JS stays untouched. Layout grammar may need reconciliation depending on suite's current shape — pending suite-Claude's next-round file export.

### What session D' will roll back

- `src/components/void-engine.css` (~8.3 KB) — text-transformer styling. Delete; not reusable for image-prompt builder layout.
- `src/components/void-engine.js` (~9.2 KB) — registry + PRNG + DOM controller for text transforms. Delete; suite app has its own controller, no port value.
- `src/void-engine/index.html` — full overwrite with suite Void Engine port wrapped in wuld.ink chrome (site header / nav / footer / page hero).
- Homepage Void card already rolled back to `data-status="forthcoming"` this turn (tag updated to "Image-prompt builder — port pending"); no further index.html change needed for the rollback step itself.

## Standalone session deliverables blocks (pre-K)

### Session D deliverables (2026-05-13)

- **`src/components/void-engine.css`** (~8.3 KB) — instrument styling: signal textarea (blood-red accent rail, mono, brutalist border, dim italic placeholder, focus-visible ring), mode radiogroup (button row with hairline borders between presets, active mode flips to accent fill), seed input (labeled tag + numeric field, "auto" placeholder when empty), transmit button (right-aligned via margin-inline-start: auto on desktop, full-width on mobile), section-rule with absolutely-positioned "TRANSMISSION" label punching through, transmission output region (accent-dim rail goes hot when transmitted), meta readout (preset · seed · char count), full mobile fallback (stacks vertically <640px), screen-reader-only utility class.
- **`src/components/void-engine.js`** (~9.2 KB) — IIFE-scoped controller. Mulberry32 seeded PRNG; xmur3 string-to-seed hash for empty-seed-input fallthrough (auto-seed becomes pure function of Signal content → reproducible without manual seed entry). Registry as Map: `register(slug, {label, transform})`. Two stubs auto-registered on boot: `null` (passthrough) and `inversion` (Array.from + reverse + join — surrogate-pair safe). Public API exposed at `window.VoidEngine` with `register`, `list`, `run`, `rehydrate`. DOM hydration: builds radio buttons from registry, wires keyboard arrow nav within radiogroup, form submit handler, Cmd/Ctrl+Enter shortcut from textarea, empty-signal handling falls back to idle state, error state on transform throw. Try/catch around `mod.transform()` so a buggy chat-authored preset can't take down the page.
- **`src/void-engine/index.html`** — placeholder `[ · ]` frame replaced with the live instrument. Page-intro paragraph in italic serif body register sets the instrument's mood without philosophical content. Inline `<script>` chat-side authoring contract documented in a trailing comment block — example registration pattern + reminder to call `VoidEngine.rehydrate()` after appending presets.
- **`src/index.html`** — homepage Void card `data-status="forthcoming"` attribute removed; card is now live-state (no `↳` prefix on the tag).

**Smoke-test results:** 6/6 PRNG + registry unit tests pass (passthrough, inversion, surrogate-pair safe inversion, content-deterministic auto-seed, explicit seed honored, PRNG same-seed reproducibility). Live HTTP server probe: void-engine page returns 200 (5128 bytes), all 6 referenced assets resolve 200, all expected structural elements present (void-engine section, signal input, modes radiogroup, transmission output, aria-live polite, void-engine.js script tag, role="radiogroup"). JS passes `node -c` syntax check. CSS braces balanced (39 open / 39 close). Note: bash mount of `index.html` shows a stale pre-session-B snapshot (mtime 00:56) so the homepage edit isn't visible to bash but IS visible to the file-tool Read — the workspace folder (which Cloudflare Pages deploys from) reflects the live edit.

**Chat-side authoring contract for Void Engine transmission modes:** SUPERSEDED by D'. The text-transformer registry contract no longer exists. The new Void Engine is the suite's image-prompt builder — modifier DB is inline `const DB=[...]` in the engine script; modifications flow via suite-side canonical → relay-doc re-export → wuld.ink port re-apply.

### Session D' deliverables (2026-05-13)

- **`src/void-engine/index.html`** (262,118 bytes / 2,007 lines) — full overwrite. Suite Void Engine canonical (`void-engine-suite-canonical.html`, 271,059 bytes, ported from `VOID_ENGINE_v5.html`) wrapped in wuld.ink chrome via four bounded transformations:
  - **Chrome wrap.** Before canonical `<body><div class="app">`: skip-link, `<header class="site-header">` with site-mark + nav (6 destinations, `aria-current="page"` on /void-engine/), `<main id="main">`. After canonical's closing `</div>` (line 547 of the post-edit file): `</main>`, `<footer class="page-footer">` (mono / blood-bordered / dim text, inline-styled with canonical's `--bdr` / `--mono` / `--mist` / `--void` vars to merge into the engine's dark register), `<script src="/components/nav.js">` for aria-current activation.
  - **Stylesheet injection.** `<link rel="stylesheet">` to `/tokens.css`, `/base.css`, `/components/nav.css` injected in head BEFORE canonical's inline `<style>` (so canonical's `:root` token names — `--void`, `--blood`, `--mono`, etc. — override nothing; canonical uses distinct names from wuld.ink's `--c-bg`, `--c-accent`, `--font-mono` and there are zero collisions). Google Fonts `preconnect` to `fonts.gstatic.com` added.
  - **Anthropic API strip per Exchange 3 B1 lock.** Removed: CSS rules `.corp-mode-row`, `.corp-mode-btn*`, `.corp-api-section*`, `.corp-api-row`, `.corp-api-note`, `.corp-key-in*`, `.corp-key-status*`, `.corp-api-badge`, `.corp-loading`, `.corp-spin`, `@keyframes spin`. HTML: `.corp-mode-row` div with LOCAL/API toggle buttons + entire `#corp-api-sec` block (key input, save/clear/status). JS: `let corpMode`, `function setCorpMode`, `function checkApiKeyStatus`, `function saveApiKey`, `function clearApiKey`, `async function runCorpusAPI`, `async function _runCorpusApiMode` (80-line API implementation). Dispatcher simplified to local-only: `var runCorpus=function(){_runCorpusLocalMode();};`. Intro paragraph re-worded to drop the "Deep mode" sentence. Strip placeholder comment retained at site for clean suite-resync. Net: 180 lines / ~7.8 KB removed from canonical baseline. Public port has zero references to `anthropic`, `sk-ant`, `api-key`, `corpMode`, `runCorpusAPI`, `_runCorpusApiMode`, `setCorpMode`, `saveApiKey`, `clearApiKey`, `checkApiKeyStatus`.
  - **ARCH_KEY localStorage rename per A4.** `const ARCH_KEY='void-engine-v5:archive'` → `const ARCH_KEY='wuld.ink:void-engine:archive'`. Surgical single-literal change. Round-trip verified offline (Node simulation of localStorage + DOM stubs): `archGetAll()` returns `[]` initially, then returns parsed array after a synthetic `setItem` to the new key.
- **`src/index.html`** — homepage Void card `data-status="forthcoming"` removed; tag updated from "Image-prompt builder — port pending" → "Analog & nihilist generative lexicon" (live state, no `↳` prefix).
- **`docs/void-engine-suite-coordination.md`** — synced to upload (Exchange 3 from suite-Claude landed). Exchange 4 reply appended: A1–A5 + B1/B2 closures, A5 carve-out for chrome integration documented, C1 new flag (file ships 222 modifier entries by 5 independent parsing methods; suite-Claude said 227 in B2 — minor delta worth suite-side audit, non-blocking).

**Logic preservation principle held.** Every engine function preserved at the implementation level: `boot`, `compile`, `loadPreset`, `_runCorpusLocalMode`, `archGetAll`/`archSave`, `doSearch`, `setCat`, `toggleNeg`, `toggleReadable`, `corpScore`, `corpTokenize`, deep scan, diagnosis modal, full local Corpus Analyzer. Only the API-mode branch was excised; local mode is untouched.

**Smoke-test results (offline, file-level — sandbox can't bind HTTP):** HTML balance 100/100 divs + 1/1 each of html/head/body/main/style + 2/2 script; UTF-8 clean (1135 trailing nulls from a python write quirk stripped post-hoc); JS parses in non-strict and strict mode (221,282 chars / 1451 lines); zero stray API identifiers via static analyzer; ARCH_KEY localStorage round-trip works in Node simulation; DB parses to 222 entries via 5 parsing methods (regex `\bid:'[^']+'`, etc.); DS parses to 222 keys; 15 categories (`Aesthetic & Texture`, `Biological / Thermodynamic`, `Camera & Process`, `Clinical Abjection`, `Color Grade`, `Compositional Grammar`, `Figure / Subject`, `Infrastructure / Ruin`, `Lighting & Atmosphere`, `Liminal Space`, `Normative / Ironic`, `Psychogenic / Dissociation`, `Runway / Video`, `Sound / Duration`, `Void / Dissolution`); structural elements (.hdr, .perm-bar, .panel, .neg-panel, .pre-row, .chips-panel, .corpus-panel, .archive-panel) all present at expected positions. Live-browser smoke test (Josiah-side): load `/void-engine/` in browser, expect: nav at top renders in Plex Mono with "Void" highlighted as current page; engine instrument header renders below in Space Mono with blood-red accent; modifier chips populate; click a preset (e.g., "Taedium Vitae") — positive prompt output should populate; localStorage inspect should show `wuld.ink:void-engine:archive` key on first archive save; no console errors; no network requests to api.anthropic.com.

### Session D'' deliverables (2026-05-13)

- **`src/void-engine/index.html`** (380,265 bytes / 4,308 lines post-port) — D' standalone port REPLACED by bundled triptych port. Source: `DUAL_ENGINE_v2.html` (383,899 bytes pre-port, suite-Claude reported 379,499 expanded ~4 KB by export transport; post-null-strip wuld.ink-side at 380,265 — see Exchange 8 E2). Six bounded transformations applied:
  - **Chrome wrap (triptych scale).** Before suite's `<div id="engine-toggle">`: skip-link, `<header class="site-header">` with site-mark + nav (6 destinations, aria-current handled by nav.js), `<main id="main">`. After the last engine wrapper + all four script tags + before `</body>`: `</main>`, `<footer class="page-footer">` (Plex Mono, opaque background `#030303` matching canonical body, blood-red return-link), `<script src="/components/nav.js">`. Toggle bar (#engine-toggle, canonical sticky position z:9990) sits below the site-header at top of `<main>`; three engine wrappers (#void-engine-wrap, #trans-engine-wrap, #sig-engine-wrap) follow as siblings inside `<main>`.
  - **Stylesheet injection.** `<link rel="stylesheet">` to `/tokens.css`, `/base.css`, `/components/nav.css` injected in head BEFORE canonical's inline `<style>` (zero `:root` token-name collisions with canonical's `--void`/`--blood`/`--mono`/`--mist`/`--bdr`/`--amber`/etc.). Google Fonts `preconnect` to `fonts.gstatic.com` added.
  - **Anthropic API strip per Exchange 3 B1.** Identical scope to D' (the API path lives entirely in Void Engine's portion of the bundle): CSS rule block (`.corp-mode-row`, `.corp-mode-btn*`, `.corp-api-section*`, `.corp-api-row`, `.corp-api-note`, `.corp-key-in*`, `.corp-key-status*`, `.corp-api-badge`, `.corp-loading`, `.corp-spin`, `@keyframes spin`), HTML (corp-mode-row buttons + entire `#corp-api-sec` div), 7 JS functions (`let corpMode`, `setCorpMode`, `checkApiKeyStatus`, `saveApiKey`, `clearApiKey`, `runCorpusAPI`, `_runCorpusApiMode`), dispatcher simplified to local-only. `corp-intro` paragraph re-worded (drop "Deep mode" sentence). Static analyzer confirms zero references to API identifiers in functional code (only in strip-site placeholder comments). Signal + Transmission unaffected — confirmed zero external surface per Exchange 7 D6.
  - **ARCH_KEY rename.** Single-literal swap `void-engine-v5:archive` → `wuld.ink:void-engine:archive`. Same D' A4 surgery. Signal Engine + Transmission have zero localStorage usage per Exchange 7 D4 — no additional renames needed.
  - **D5=α hash-route shim.** 22 lines of JS appended to the toggle-script block (`<script>` at lines 922-988), after `switchEngine` definition. `_hashToEngine()` parses `location.hash`: `#sig`/`#signal` → 'sig', `#trans`/`#transmission` → 'trans', `#void` or bare → 'void', else null. `_applyHashRoute()` calls `switchEngine(target)` if non-null. Listeners: `hashchange` + `DOMContentLoaded` (or immediate if document already past loading). Suite-side standalone Dual Engine V2 untouched (the shim is harmless when no URL routing is in effect). Decision rationale per Exchange 7 D5: URL semantics belong to the umbrella, not the instrument.
  - **D7=β Transmission canvas full-bleed under chrome.** CSS rules appended to end of canonical inline `<style>` block: `#trans-engine-wrap.active { position:fixed; inset:0; z-index:0; width:100vw; height:100vh; }` hoists the wrap out of normal flow when Transmission is active. HUD offsets: `#t-corner-tl` top:`calc(104px + 16px)` (clears site-header + toggle bar bands); `#t-corner-br` + `#t-hud` bottom:`calc(50px + 16px)` (clears footer band). Site-header + page-footer get `z-index:9991` to backstop the inline z:20. `body:has(#trans-engine-wrap.active) { overflow: hidden; }` prevents the 100vh wrap from pushing document scroll. Decision rationale per Exchange 7 D7: constraining canvas to chrome-aware viewport (α) breaks the threshold-crossing argument from A5; floating it full-bleed under opaque chrome bands preserves the suite posture (chrome-as-frame, transmission-as-void).
- **`src/index.html`** — homepage Void card updated: label `04 · Instrument` → `04 · Triptych`; tag `"Analog & nihilist generative lexicon"` → `"Lexicon · signal · transmission"`. Triptych now reflected in the umbrella index.

- **`setup-git.ps1` (ASCII, ~110 lines)** — bootstrap PowerShell script at repo root. Idempotent one-shot local git init+commit. Six-stage flow: (1) Wipe prior `.git/` if present (Remove-Item with attribute-clearing pass + `cmd /c rd /s /q` fallback for OneDrive locks); (2) Remove stray sandbox artifacts (`wuld-ink-deploy-*.zip`, `ziGq6fkD`, `ziCwRmw0`, any `^zi[A-Za-z0-9]{6}$` pattern); (3) `git init -b main`; (4) `git config user.name/email` (local scope); (5) `git add .` + verify no strays staged + spot-check of expected files; (6) Commit via four `-m` flags (no here-strings — PS 5.1 parser unsafe with UTF-8 BOM stripping). NOT using `$ErrorActionPreference = "Stop"` because native git stderr (e.g., `fatal: not a git repository` probes) trips PS's NativeCommandError handling under Stop mode. Manual `$LASTEXITCODE` check after `git init` and `git commit`. Pre-flag in comment block explains why this script exists (OneDrive corruption + PS 5.1 parser brittleness). Lives in the repo at root; harmless if it stays. Removable in a future commit if desired.
- **Cloudflare Pages project rebuilt as Git-connected** — old direct-upload `wuld-ink` project deleted; new project created via dedicated `/workers-and-pages/create/pages` URL (NOT the unified `/workers-and-pages/create` which only creates Workers projects). **Prerequisite gotcha #1:** Cloudflare blocks project deletion until custom domains detach — had to manually remove wuld.ink + www.wuld.ink first via Custom domains tab → `…` menu → Remove domain → confirm (modal warns "The CNAME record pointing to your project will be removed"). **Prerequisite gotcha #2:** Per safety rules, project deletion itself (a permanent destructive operation) requires explicit user action — I prepared the modal but Josiah completed the typed-confirmation + click. **Build config:** framework preset None, build command empty, build output directory `src`, root directory blank, no env vars. Project name reused → reclaimed `wuld-ink.pages.dev` hostname. First Git deploy from `0ac009a` succeeded (build env init 3s + clone 2s + build 5s + deploy ~15s = ~25s total).
- **Custom domains re-attached** — wuld.ink + www.wuld.ink via Custom domains tab → Set up a custom domain → enter domain → Continue → Confirm DNS record (Cloudflare auto-creates `CNAME @ wuld-ink.pages.dev` for apex and `CNAME www wuld-ink.pages.dev` for www) → Activate domain. Both initially showed "Verifying" status with a "Complete DNS setup" expandable link. One click on each "Check DNS records" button flipped both to Active with SSL enabled. ~10 min total downtime in the detach-to-reattach gap. Apex CNAME auto-create works because Cloudflare supports CNAME flattening at apex.
- **Auto-deploy verified end-to-end** — sentinel empty commit `c239c9c` (`git commit --allow-empty -m "Sentinel: verify Pages Git-deploy auto-trigger (E3, 2026-05-13)"` + `git push`). Cloudflare webhook detected within seconds; auto-built and deployed to `4eede190.wuld-ink.pages.dev`. - **Process retrospective for future Cowork sessions:** (1) When wiring Pages → Git, go directly to `https://dash.cloudflare.com/<account>/workers-and-pages/create/pages` — do NOT trust the `/pages/new` URL (redirects to unified flow) or the top-level `/workers-and-pages/create` page (creates Workers, not Pages). (2) When OneDrive folder + Linux sandbox bash interact, expect the sandbox to fail at file-unlink + atomic-write operations the OneDrive sync indexer touches; PowerShell on Windows is the right execution surface for git ops in OneDrive folders. (3) GitHub will block any first push if commit author = your private primary email + email-privacy is on — pre-set local `user.email` to the noreply form OR be ready to amend+force-push the first commit. (4) Cloudflare Pages project conversion from direct-upload → Git-connected is NOT supported — only delete+recreate. Plan for ~10 min downtime if custom domains are involved.

- **Item 1 — Homepage polish.** `.site-mark` `font-weight: 700` dropped from `src/components/nav.css` so the wordmark and nav links share the same family AND weight (size — 20px wordmark vs 14px nav strip — now carries the hierarchy alone, per the spec "reconcile to same family at different sizes only"). Cover handles row removed entirely from `src/index.html`: the `WULD · AnomicIndividual87 · Evilis Anihilis Uls` line was decorative noise; WULD redundant with the title. Cover collapses to bracketed title + slab rule + INDEX↓ descent affordance. **INDEX↓ axis fix** shipped via a `visibility:hidden` arrow-balancer span placed left of "Index" so the visible word centers on the page axis with the arrow as right-decoration. Diagnosis: the prior inline-flex centered the UNIT (Index + arrow + gap) as a whole, which optically pushed "Index" left of the title's centerline because "Index" is wider than "↓". Balancer-span pattern: insert an aria-hidden symmetric ghost of the trailing arrow on the leading side; CSS `visibility:hidden` + `pointer-events:none` + `user-select:none` make it inert. `.cover-descent` constraints also matched to `.cover-mark-block` (max-width + margin-inline:auto + width:100%) for centerline parity at all viewport widths. Stranded `.cover-handles` / `.cover-handles span` / `.cover-handles .sep` CSS rules removed from the homepage `<style>` block.

- **Lessons logged for future Cowork sessions:**
  1. **Re-scope at session start when source files contradict shell assumptions.** Session B's three-section audio scaffold was built before the actual recording existed. The recording landed as one file. Surfacing the mismatch upfront + rewriting the architecture (not the audio) was the right move — pretending the scaffold held would have required Josiah to manually split the WAV at fictional section boundaries.
  2. **WAV → MP3 conversion is mandatory before R2 upload.** ElevenLabs raw WAV is ~10 MB/min; essay-length readings hit 100-300 MB. 96k mono MP3 lands at ~700 KB/min, ~50x smaller, fine fidelity for spoken-word. Parallel ffmpeg in sandbox is fast (3 files / ~65 min total audio / 22s wall when backgrounded).
  3. **Sandbox `du -h` reports 0 bytes on OneDrive-mounted files even when bytes exist.** Mount-layer block-counting quirk. Use `ls -la` or `stat -c "%s"` for real byte counts.
  4. **R2 bucket-size metric lags actual state.** Post-upload bucket-size displayed "0 B" while Class A ops counter showed 8 successful writes and HEAD verified the object cleanly. Trust HEAD + ops counters over the bucket-size metric for immediate verification.
  5. **R2 dashboard folder drag-drop preserves path structure.** Dragging the `essays/` folder onto bucket root → object key landed at `essays/sanguinolentum-vestigium/full.mp3` cleanly. No need to navigate into synthetic folders first or specify prefix in the upload dialog. Cheapest path for multi-file uploads when audio uploads are one-off; wrangler still wins for frequent uploads.

**Lessons logged for future Cowork sessions:**
1. **When session work adds a new mid-session decision (like the merch question), wrap it in AskUserQuestion + lock the direction before implementation.** The Linktree-vs-direct decision was non-obvious (had genuine reasoning on both sides); building first then asking later would have risked re-work.
2. **Sandbox `cp` works in OneDrive paths even when `mv`/`rm` are blocked.** `cp` writes a new file (no unlink), so OneDrive's sync indexer doesn't fight it. Useful for the audio-staging folder-preservation pattern when the source MP3 is flat and the R2 destination needs nested path.
3. **`.audio-intro` SV→glossary promotion paid off immediately** — the second-mounting case (Alogical) only needs HTML markup, no CSS duplication. Pattern: when a session-N feature ships inline `<style>` on a specific page, promote to component CSS the FIRST time a sibling surface wants the same feature, not the third. Component CSS earns its keep on the second use, not the second-and-half.
4. **For external link-outs in the homepage grid, use `target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"` and signal externality in the tag text** ("external" suffix on tag clears the visitor's expectation without needing a glyph). Consistent with the Watch card's `YouTube · WULD Incorporated` tag pattern but explicit-external where Watch is internal-page-with-external-thumbs.

### Session J deliverables (2026-05-13 micro)

Same-day as G + post-G + H + I. Four workstreams shipped clean: (1) cover-axis fix triggered mid-session by Josiah's aesthetic screenshot; (2) library-Claude Exchange 3 response intake (LIGHT — all confirmations + threshold defined + relay round closed); (3) Amazon book link locked and 09th grid card shipped (Malgré Tout); (4) footer propagation across 13 shells via shared `/components/footer.css`.

- **Cover-axis fix (session-start aesthetic note from Josiah).** Screenshot showed the W.U.L.D. INCORPORATED video sitting visibly right-of-axis within its bracketed frame; subhead `WORTHLESS · USELESS · LIFELESS · DEAD` + INDEX↓ rendered correctly on page axis, confirming the bug was local to the cover-mark video element. Diagnosis: `.cover-mark--video` is an h1 with `display:flex; width:100%; max-width:50rem;` but **no `margin-inline:auto`**. Block-level h1 doesn't honor parent's `text-align:center` for its own box positioning when capped under parent width — it defaults to the start edge. Parent `.cover-mark-block` is wider than 50rem (capped at `--w-max`), so the h1 sat left-of-center within it. Flex `justify-content:center` correctly centered brackets+video INSIDE the h1, but the h1 itself was offset. Subhead + INDEX↓ rendered correctly because they're text within text-align:center'd block-flow (not flex containers). Fix: one-line `margin-inline: auto` addition to `.cover-mark--video` rules, with inline comment explaining the axis-fix rationale for future debug-readers. **Post-deploy patch (same day, post-session-J commit):** structural centering shipped clean (curl-verified 5/5 `margin-inline:auto` rules in deployed HTML; pre-J figure-shifted-right is now figure-centered). Initial follow-on tune shipped + reverted: max-width 50rem → 32rem → 50rem. Josiah preferred the original frame size; the bracket-hug-the-figure problem turned out to be a misread of the actual visual issue — the real misalignment was the cover SUBHEAD (`Worthless · Useless · Lifeless · Dead`), not the video frame. **Subhead root cause logged:** `base.css` applies `max-width: var(--w-prose)` to ALL `<p>` elements as a global prose-readability default. The subhead is a `<p>`, so its box was capped at prose-width (~65ch) — but without `margin-inline:auto`, the constrained box sat at the start edge of `.cover-mark-block` (block elements default to start, not center). `text-align:center` centered the text within the narrow left-edge box, NOT within the full parent. The slab rule (`<hr>`) and INDEX↓ (`<p>` with its own `margin-inline:auto`) didn't have this issue. Fix: one-line `margin-inline: auto` on `.cover-subhead` with inline comment explaining the base.css interaction. **Lesson logged for future Cowork:** when a global rule in `base.css` constrains an element type's box (max-width, max-content, etc.), per-component CSS for that element type must add `margin-inline:auto` to center the constrained box — text-align:center alone only centers content WITHIN the box, not the box within its parent. Audit existing `<p>` instances on the homepage for similar latent issues (cover-descent has its own margin-inline:auto from session G fix, so it's already safe).

- **Library-Claude Exchange 3 response intake.** Library-Claude's Exchange 3 reply landed via upload at session start; triaged as LIGHT (all confirmations, no material-shift ratifications). Replaced the placeholder section in `docs/library-claude-coordination.md` with the filled response: **Coda (c) CONFIRM** + **VAR (d) CONFIRM** + **why-not-suicide (c) CONFIRM**. Threshold answer for VAR material-shift flags defined per-shift-class: changes to *what* VAR claims (mechanism diagnosis / archetype-conditional space / MAP/DEP graph positioning) = **material → FLAG**; prose-shape and depth-toggle wording changes = **stylistic → NO FLAG**; neighbor-objection recharacterization = **CONDITIONAL** (default no, atypical-backdoor revisions cross the bar). Threshold shape: *finer-grained than "MAJOR canon bump only"* — reads off the mutation, not the version bump. **Flagging cadence:** per-session-close via a compact one-line marker appended to library-side's `session_log` (form: `[WULD-FLAG: VAR mechanism recharacterized via c8-cascade-ord-5]`). Library-Claude closed the relay round with no new forced question; the previously-tracked "Exchange 4 question owed by library-side re: VAR notification threshold" is now resolved. Subsequent coordination triggers from wuld.ink-side as material flags accumulate or as integration milestone-chain advances (stable-tag → subdomain provisioning → F+ slot opens).

- **Amazon book link locked + 09th grid card shipped.** Confirmed via AskUserQuestion that ASIN `B0GZ18XVTD` = **"Malgré Tout: A Guide to Nothingness"** — a distinct published book separate from `/book/`'s in-development hybrid compendium. Option (b) from session-I deferred decision was the right call (distinct artifact = its own card, not a replacement for /book/ or an inline cross-link). Replaced the `.destination-placeholder` div at grid slot 09 with a new external-link card pattern-matched to Wares: `09 · Treatise / Malgré Tout / A Guide to Nothingness · Amazon · external` → `https://www.amazon.com/dp/B0GZ18XVTD` with `target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"`. Label "Treatise" picked register-tight over neutral alternatives ("Volume" / "Standalone" / "Published") — carries philosophical weight matching Josiah's register, distinguishes from "05 · Long-work" which targets the in-development compendium. Grid is now 9 actual destinations, no placeholder slot remaining. `.destination-placeholder` CSS rules retained as dead-code (cheap to keep, useful if a 10th destination ever opens; rules currently don't apply to any element).

- **Footer propagation to 13 shells via shared component CSS.** Promoted homepage `.home-footer` rules to NEW `/components/footer.css` (~60 lines, single canonical source for `.page-footer` + `.page-footer-inner` + `.copyright strong` + `.disclaimer-pending` + `.disclaimer-pending::before`). Canonical class is `.page-footer` (renamed from `.home-footer` on homepage + from `.site-footer` on templates/essay.html). Per session-I lesson 3: component CSS earns its keep on the second use — at 13 surfaces wanting the same pattern, promotion is amply justified. All 13 shells now consume the shared stylesheet via `<link rel="stylesheet" href="/components/footer.css">` in head, with the canonical body pattern (`<span class="copyright">` + `<span class="disclaimer-pending">`).

  - **13-file roster:** 9 page-footer shells (`index.html` home + `essays/index` + `essays/sanguinolentum-vestigium` + `argument-library` + `book` + `blog` + `glossary/index` + `watch` + `void-engine` [special, see below]), 1 site-footer template (`templates/essay`), 3 glossary files with NO previous footer (`glossary/_template` + `glossary/alogical-isness` + `glossary/contextus-claudit` — footer ADDED between `</main>` and script tags). Scaffold-era footer text (`WULD · wuld.ink · 2026–` + `Cloudflare Pages + R2`) gone from every file. Smoke-checked via grep: 0 occurrences of scaffold text, 31 occurrences of canonical `copyright|disclaimer-pending` across 13 expected files.
  - **Void-engine special case (D'' triptych chrome).** Footer keeps its inline-styled chrome (`#030303` bg, `#8a847b` text, `#2a2a2a` border, centered single-line text) per session-D'' chrome-wrap discipline — blends with canonical triptych register, NOT umbrella tokens. Linking footer.css there would have been a no-op visually (inline-style specificity wins) AND introduced subtle conflict risk with the canonical inline `<style>` block. Decision: SKIP footer.css link to void-engine, just update the footer body text to: `© Josiah S. Cooper · 2010–2026 · all rights reserved · return to index`. The disclaimer-pending pointer is umbrella-only register (not instrument-mode-fit); return-to-index affordance preserved as the meaningful umbrella signpost in the triptych context.
  - **Watch one-off.** Footer had a `<span><a href="/" ...>← Return to index</a></span>` second span instead of the scaffold `Cloudflare Pages + R2` (different pattern variant from session G). Replaced with the canonical copyright + disclaimer pattern; return-to-index removed (site-header logo already provides homepage navigation; redundant in footer).
  - **Templates/essay.html (`.site-footer` third class-name variant).** Renamed `.site-footer` → `.page-footer` in HTML body, removed inline `.site-footer*` rule block, added footer.css link. Now consistent with canonical pattern.
  - **Deferred cleanup.** Inline `.page-footer*` rule blocks still live in the 8 standard shells' `<style>` tags as dead code (~20 lines × 8 = ~160 lines total). Linked footer.css comes after the inline rules in head source order, so the linked stylesheet wins; the inline rules are dead but harmless. Removable in a future micro-session via parallel Edits; not blocking.

**Files touched (session J):** `src/components/footer.css` (NEW, ~60 lines), `src/index.html` (cover-axis fix + footer.css link + dead-rule removal + class rename in HTML + Malgré Tout 09th grid card), 9 page-shell HTML files (footer.css link + footer body rewrite), `src/templates/essay.html` (link + inline-rule removal + class rename + body rewrite), 3 glossary files (link + footer HTML insert between main + scripts), 1 void-engine (footer body text only — skipped link). **15 files modified + 1 new = 16 total.** Same-day commit waves expected: deliverables first (16 files), docs second (CLAUDE.md + memory).

**Tool-budget retrospective (session J):** Projected 30-50 at session start with relay-doc-as-light triage; actual ~55 by close. Slightly over projection — the watch one-off (different pattern variant required separate Edit), the void-engine special-case handling, and the cover-axis mid-session aesthetic interrupt added ~5 unplanned calls. Within ceiling. Pre-flag discipline held: warned at session start about footer propagation being the bulk-spend item; that bore out (footer propagation accounted for ~30 calls of the total).

**Lessons logged for future Cowork sessions:**
1. **Mid-session screenshots from Josiah → triage immediately, fix inline if fast.** The cover-axis fix was a one-line CSS edit shippable in the same turn as the message; deferring it would have created context-switching overhead and risked forgetting. The system-reminder pattern enforces this discipline ("you MUST address the user's message").
2. **Grep output escaping is not byte-faithful to the file.** Watch's footer had `href="/"` in the actual file but grep rendered it as `href="\"` (backslash escape). Copy-pasting grep output into Edit's `old_string` failed string-match. Always Read the file directly when Edit string-match fails — grep is for locating, not for copy-pasting source bytes.
3. **Dead CSS accumulation is acceptable short-term debt when promoting to component.** Removing inline duplicates costs N edits per file (where N = shells); leaving them as dead code (~160 lines total across 8 files) costs zero visual impact + buys ~8 edits worth of tool budget. The right move when budget pressure is real and visual outcomes match between source-order-wins-anyway alternatives. Sweep can be its own micro-session.
4. **When a shared component diverges by design on one surface (like void-engine's triptych chrome), don't extend the component there.** Linking the shared stylesheet to a surface that overrides everything inline is cognitive noise + carries subtle conflict risk. Component CSS is for surfaces that share register; surfaces that diverge by design get treated as their own case.
5. **Label-picking for new homepage grid cards.** Six register-tight options considered for the 09th card: "Treatise" (chosen — philosophical weight, distinguishes from "Long-work"), "Volume" (too neutral), "Standalone" (relation-descriptor, weaker than category), "Published" (plain), "Manifeste" (matches French title but obscures the umbrella's English-default chrome), "Tome" (pretentious-without-payoff). Pattern: pick the label that descripts CATEGORY/MODE (like "Long-form" / "Reference" / "Vocabulary") not the artifact-name or relation-to-other-works.

**Parallel-safe carry-forwards still pending (not shipped this turn — mention-only):** Footer dead-CSS sweep across 8 shells (micro-session); intro-stamp max-width tune-up on cover if 50rem reads off in live deploy; Architecture-of-Moral-Disaster MP3 placement decision (new essay shell vs watch-card audio embed); Alogical Isness/Architecture WAV→MP3 staged at `_audio-staging/` ready for placement; SV inline-passage-alignment markers (chat-side authorship as audio-prose annotation lands); `library.wuld.ink` subdomain provisioning waits for library audit close + stable tag v3.7.0+; F+ editorial library extraction (coda, 2 canonical objection long-forms, static Map 1 frame on "about the library") — runs AFTER library audit closes; D2 flash card scaffolding (still awaits Josiah's content + tech decisions); blog short-form FB-post curation; book card decisions about /book/ as compendium-in-development vs Amazon-pointer.

Multiple-Claude-instances-converging signals are stronger than single-Claude judgments. (iii) **Token-budget pre-flagging as a discipline** — Josiah's "we might need to do this in a few" pacing instruction was the right framing; K4 limited to triage + Author URL prevented the half-finished-vessel-work outcome that would have occurred under HEAVY scope. (iv) **OneDrive sandbox mount staleness can manifest mid-session** — uploads/ + docs/ both worked via bash early in K4 then went null-byte sometime around the cp-corruption incident; file-tool path (Anthropic file API → Windows file system direct) is the durable fallback when this happens. (v) **Coord-doc relay file restoration via Josiah-side action** — if uploads don't persist between sessions, the only way to ship a clean library/suite Exchange N reply append is: (A) Josiah re-uploads at K5 start, OR (B) Josiah saves coord-doc files locally on his computer + Cowork file-tool Reads them next session. Pre-flagging (B) as the durable option for cross-session relay-doc continuity. **Two-commit pattern at session close** (per session H lesson): deliverables commit first (`/book/index.html` Author URL update + `docs/book-claude-coordination.md` Exchange 3 reply append + .gitignore if needed), docs commit second (CLAUDE.md + memory file + MEMORY.md hook).

**`<p>` margin-inline:auto audit closed clean.** Foundation reads of `src/base.css` confirmed the global `p { max-width: var(--w-prose) }` rule applies to ALL `<p>` elements as prose-readability default. Audit: this only causes latent positioning bugs when the `<p>` lives inside a `text-align:center` parent — block-level elements default to start-edge placement under max-width caps, and `text-align:center` only centers content WITHIN the box. Surveyed `<p>` instances across homepage + shells: `.lede` (left-aligned prose inside `.page`, correct), `.audio-intro-note` (left-aligned inside `.essay-body`, correct), `.entry-placeholder` glossary bodies (left-aligned inside `.entry-body`, correct), `.book-section-placeholder` book bodies (left-aligned inside `.book-section`, correct). **Lessons logged for future Cowork sessions:**

1. **Baton intake = AskUserQuestion-on-architectural-signals before any vessel work.** The session K prompt warned that prior-K stuck at MEDIUM triage; my path was: ingest baton → confirm triage → surface architectural signal → AskUserQuestion on the implications → start work. If I'd ingested baton + started rebuilding /book/ on guess, the (i)/(ii)/(iii) decision would have surfaced as rework, not pre-work. AskUserQuestion-driven lock pays off most on the architectural-signal turns where multiple coherent paths exist.

2. **Promote-to-component on second instance.** Session I promoted `.audio-intro` from SV inline to shared glossary.css after SV+Alogical wanted it. Session K's new Alogically Is essay shell duplicates SV's inline essay CSS verbatim — that's the second use of the SV shell pattern. Future micro-session candidate: promote SV's inline essay CSS (`.essay`, `.essay-header`, `.essay-meta`, `.essay-body`, `.section-rule`, `.prose-placeholder`, `.audio-intro` already promoted) to `/components/essay.css`. Flagged but not shipped — second instance is the right threshold but not blocking.

3. **Foundation reads of adjacent surfaces catch serendipitous cross-links.** `/watch/` already had the Anfractuous Aporia video card (ID `ITUWd1vzNRQ`) from session G's facade rebuild. Reading watch's surface during session-K foundation parallel reads surfaced this for free — the new Anfractuous glossary entry's "Appears in" list got the watch cross-link without an additional scrape or chat-side ask. Lesson: when scaffolding a new entry, foundation-read sibling surfaces (watch/, essays/, /book/) for existing references to the term before writing the "Appears in" list.

4. **Audio architecture triage by reading register + duration, not source slot.** Session I mounted the 35:54 Alogical Isness audio on the glossary entry shell. Session K reclassified: 35:54 = essay-format (full reading), belongs in `/essays/`; glossary entries hold brief term explanations (1-2 min summaries at most). Pattern locked for future audio additions: brief glossary-format = glossary slot; full essay reading = essays slot; book chapter narration = `/book/` audio-adaptation strip. Audio-architecture decisions need this triage layer between content shape and slot shape — duration + reading register are the diagnostic axes.

The pattern: per-decision, identify whose call it is, route accordingly. Don't AskUserQuestion on book-Claude's content-shape decisions; don't relay-defer on Josiah's umbrella architecture. Misrouting either direction wastes turns.

# Session narratives moved at K22 trim (2026-05-15)

### Session K12 (2026-05-14 micro)

**K12 (2026-05-14 micro, day after K10/K11):** Cowork-internal forensics — live `.git/index.lock` inspection + root-cause narrowing per screenshot item (6). AskUserQuestion at session start locked scope: pivot from dry repo-audit to live-lock forensics + recovery (screenshot item (7) trim deferred to K13 per recommendation). Diagnostic-first opening surfaced critical state: (a) `.git/index.lock` IS PRESENT (0-byte, mtime 2026-05-15 00:42 UTC ≈ K11 close window, 6th-recurrence sentinel); (b) `git fsck` reports "bad index file sha1 signature / fatal: index file corrupt" — binary-level corruption deeper than K10's null-sha1 D+?? pattern; (c) 9 null-sha1 phantom entries in index (K10 carry-forward unresolved); (d) working-tree drift on CLAUDE.md (-25 lines), library-coord-doc (CRLF flip carry-forward), black-box (5751 vs HEAD 2383 bytes — pre-K8 state somehow restored). Five workstreams shipped. (1) **Forensic capture closes (6) candidate set.** Repo-side root-cause ruled OUT (no hooks, no `.gitattributes`, vanilla Windows-defaults `.git/config` — `filemode=false`, `ignorecase=true`, `symlinks=false`, no autocommit/autopack/LFS/smudge filter). In-sandbox concurrent-process ruled OUT (PID forensic: only sandbox bash + transient subshells in `/proc`, no persistent git process touching repo). Lock-churn ruled OUT (mtime stable across 1s probe; earlier ls-vs-xxd flake was sandbox-mount cache desync, not real create+delete cycle). Interrupted-PS-recovery theory WEAKENED — reflog shows `1d58bc8 HEAD@{0}: reset: moving to HEAD` confirming K11's `git reset HEAD` ran to completion (reflog entry only writes on successful operations; an interrupted reset would not appear). Strongest remaining candidates narrowed to: (i) out-of-band Windows-side process (Defender/AV scan + re-lock cycle, IDE git integration like VS Code, file watcher); (ii) Anthropic sandbox session-boundary hook touching `.git/index*` post-PS-completion (no evidence visible, speculative); (iii) some Windows-side automation not yet enumerated. **Sandbox path BLOCKED for clearance** — `rm -fv .git/index.lock` returns "Operation not permitted" (Windows file lock blocks Linux unlink); `git read-tree HEAD` fails with "Unable to create '.git/index.lock': File exists / Another git process seems to be running". Sandbox forensic capabilities exhausted; the root-cause question moves out of Cowork-side investigation surface to Windows-side observability (Sysinternals Handle / Process Explorer / Defender exclusion test). (2) **Conclusion for screenshot item (6): PS recovery stays the durable pattern.** Repo-side and sandbox-side root-causes both eliminated. Out-of-band Windows-side mechanism not isolable from Cowork-side. The Windows-side recovery PROCESS can be hardened — idempotent, atomic (no partial state if interrupted), transactional (verify each step before next), interruption-survivable. **`recover-git.ps1` shipped at repo root** alongside the E3-era `setup-git.ps1` — handles all known recovery cases: (a) clear `.git/index.lock` via PS `Remove-Item -Force` (Windows-owned process unlinks own lock cleanly), (b) verify lock cleared via `Test-Path`, (c) detect index corruption via `git fsck --no-reflogs`, (d) if corrupt, run `git read-tree HEAD` (lower-level than `git reset HEAD` — rebuilds index from HEAD tree without disturbing working tree), (e) verify post-rebuild integrity via fsck + `git status --short`, (f) emit diagnostic if any step fails. Idempotent: re-running is safe (each step short-circuits if state already correct). Interruption-survivable: if PS terminal closes mid-operation, the partial-state is detectable by the next run (lock check + fsck check + null-sha1 entry count). (3) **Drifted-tracked-file restore from HEAD via `git show HEAD:$f > $f` bypass.** This sandbox-side write does NOT touch git index (no lock interaction). Three files restored: CLAUDE.md (296 lines, K10-narrative-complete state), `docs/library-claude-coordination.md` (LF line endings restored — K8.5 CRLF flip carry-forward closed), `src/glossary/black-box-of-inaccessibility/index.html` (2383 bytes, K8 redirect-stub state restored). Pattern locks for K9+K10+K12 drift-restore protocol — durable across Windows-mount staleness, works for text + binary alike (git's blob canonicalization handles both). (4) **K11 working-tree state LOST.** Reflog confirms no K11 commit ever happened (most recent reflog: K10 docs `1d58bc8` then successful reset). K11's `docs/book-claude-coordination.md` Exchange 4 append (P2 `/preface/` follow-up + P3 Mementos: Tucson + Desk authorization + verbatim text request) is gone — drift consumed the working-tree changes between K11 close and K12 open. Carry-forward for K13: reconstruct Exchange 4 from K11's intent (text not preserved Cowork-side) OR await Josiah chat-side reconstruction. Cowork CAN scaffold the Exchange 4 frame (Section A/B/C/D headers) but the content (P2 reply + P3 authorization paragraph) is content-shaped per the Cowork-builds-vessels boundary. (5) **K12 docs:** this CLAUDE.md narrative + memory file fresh-write + MEMORY.md hook update + arc table row. **Tool budget retrospective:** Projected ~30-40 calls at session start; actual ~30 by close (under projection). Diagnostic-first opening saved ~5 calls (caught drift state in first batch alongside lock state). AskUserQuestion-driven scope-lock prevented ~10 calls of half-executing dry audit before pivoting. **`<p>` margin-inline:auto audit:** N/A this turn (no vessel work; forensics + recovery + docs only). **K12 lessons logged:** (i) **Live-lock forensic surface is higher signal than dry root-cause audit.** Lock present at session-open is rare — usually session-boundary recovery clears it. K12 caught lock in-state + ran sandbox-side clearance attempt + read index integrity via fsck. Forensic narrowed candidate set from 5 to 2-3 hypotheses in one session. (ii) **Sandbox cannot rm Windows-locked files** — confirmed across K7+K8+K9+K10+K12 (six+ recurrences). Out-of-band Windows-side recovery is the durable pattern; the only Cowork-side lever is hardening the recovery script. (iii) **`git show HEAD:$f > $f` bypass is the durable drift-restore pattern** — locked across K9+K10+K12. (iv) **Reflog as forensic surface** — reflog confirmed K11 reset succeeded, ruling out interrupted-recovery theory. Future sessions: read reflog early in forensic to constrain root-cause theories. (v) **K11 working-tree drift consumed uncommitted content-shaped work** — book-coord Exchange 4 append lost. **DURABLE LESSON: commit working-tree changes IMMEDIATELY after authoring sandbox-side; do NOT defer all commits to end-of-session.** The drift pattern makes deferred commits unsafe when the lock + corruption can recur post-recovery. Per-deliverable mid-session commit (when lock state permits) is the safer interleave; two-commit close pattern continues to hold for clean sessions but should NOT be relied on as the sole safety net. (vi) **CLAUDE.md size watch:** ~145K / ~300 lines post-K12 narrative add (~3-5 KB added this turn). No process in the system dump holds a handle to `.git\index.lock` specifically. `explorer.exe pid 11628` holds two FOLDER-level handles to `C:\Users\y_m_a\Projects\wuld-ink` (file-system-watcher / breadcrumb cache, proximate but not lock-relevant). `cowork-svc.exe pid 9700` shows `<unable to open process>` — handle.exe (even elevated) couldn't enumerate the privileged Cowork service handles (unprovable but suspicious). Zero handles to any `.git\` subpath, zero IDE git-integration candidates (no VS Code / JetBrains / Sublime / Git Credential Manager). All always-running daemon candidates RULED OUT by enumeration. **Conclusion: a process creates the lock during a git operation + dies before unlocking.** Strongest remaining candidate: Cowork sandbox session-boundary teardown — `cowork-svc.exe` itself or some Anthropic-side hook touches `.git/index*` on shutdown, dies before releasing. Definitive proof would require Sysinternals Process Monitor (Procmon) trace logging filesystem writes to `.git\` during a session-close cycle — heavier scope than today's; deferred until Josiah opts-in. **Operational outcome: recover-git.ps1 stays the durable pattern.** Orphan-stale locks clear via `Remove-Item -Force` cleanly (no live owner contention). Remaining candidate set: out-of-band Windows-side process, with `cowork-svc.exe` session-boundary teardown the leading suspicion (unprovable from handle.exe alone; Procmon would close). Negative results inform; investigation isn't free but scope-lockable per session. (ii) **handle.exe path-arg discipline** — when running with target path, expect filtered output (`<process>.exe pid: NNNN ... <matching handle>` or `No matching handles found`). The full system dump Josiah pasted means either no path arg was passed OR the path didn't substring-match any open handle. Either reading lands the same conclusion (no live process holds the lock), but next iteration: pre-flag the expected output shape so Josiah recognizes match-vs-no-match signal at-a-glance. (iii) **Discreet anchor-page pointer pattern locks** — K3 `.frame-pointer` aside (mono label + accent-bordered single-sentence body in /glossary/ header pointing at /frame/) established the precedent; K14 `.cover-preface-pointer` extends to homepage cover area pointing at /preface/. Anchor pages (frame, preface) get DISCREET pointers from related surfaces; destinations get grid cards. Pattern reinforces; no third anchor-page-pointer surface is currently scoped, but the formal rule holds for future additions. (iv) **Subagent delegation for >32K-token text manipulation** (K8 lesson re-validated for second time). 106 KB Status paragraph regex-split + chunk classification + dual-file write handled in one delegated turn (~16 subagent tool-uses internal, 1 main-context call). Pattern durable for CLAUDE.md size-watch trims; next trim threshold projected ~K20 if narrative growth holds K-session pace. (v) **Per-deliverable mid-session commit (K12 amendment) deferred this session** because the lock-investigation recovery cycle ran in parallel — committing pre-recovery wasn't possible (locked index), and the session's vessel-scope was light enough that two-commit close pattern remained safe. K12 amendment applies when (a) recovery state is stable mid-session AND (b) vessel scope is heavy enough that drift-loss risk warrants per-deliverable commits. K14 met neither; close-pattern returned. (vi) **Tool budget pre-flag held** — projected 30-40 / actual ~32 = within ceiling. Subagent saved direct-Edit cost on the trim; handle.exe output was pasted into context but didn't cost extra tool calls; AskUserQuestion-driven scope-lock prevented expansion. (vii) **Failed-commit staging persistence** — when a `git commit` errors mid-attempt (PS quoting bug, broken multi-`-m` invocation, etc.), prior `git add` staging does NOT roll back. Subsequent `git add` calls compound on the persisted index. First successful commit absorbs the union — which is how K14's single `4f84fa2` absorbed all three deliverables (cover pointer + trim + narrative) across what was originally planned as three separate commits. Discipline: if you want the eventual commit shape to differ from cumulative staged state, `git reset` explicitly before retry. Otherwise accept union-absorption (K14's net state was correct, just bundled differently than planned). (viii) **PowerShell multi-`-m` empty-middle quoting bug** — `git commit -m "subject" -m "" -m "body"` on PS 5.1 trips the parser on the empty middle argument (parsed as terminator, not pass-through). Result: silent commit failure or malformed message. **K15+ commit discipline:** single short `-m "summary"` per commit by default; for multi-paragraph bodies, PS here-string `-m @"..."@` or stdin (`git commit --file=-`). Avoids the empty-middle pattern entirely. Adds to the E3-era PS-discipline ledger (no `Stop` mode on native git stderr, ASCII-only commit messages, OneDrive null-byte watch on writes). **K15 carry-forwards (mention-only):** **Procmon trace investigation** if `cowork-svc.exe` candidate needs closure (heavier; Josiah opts-in — would require operator-side Sysinternals Procmon setup + capture filter on `.git\` directory writes during a session-close cycle; durable forensic evidence for the last-remaining candidate). Mementos: *Grey* verbatim text (separate book-Claude follow-up OR chat-side). Naming-divergence resolution (`/preface/` "structural pessimism" vs K5 umbrella SP→SA rename — Josiah's call; cross-Claude register pluralism per K4 lock preserves the divergence as feature by default). Mementos lede candidate authorization (K4 F4 *"A memento is a thing one keeps when one has lost the argument for keeping it."* — narrow K11 scope held; lede activation needs separate authorization). `.entry-alias` CSS promote-to-component (N=2 alias-note threshold; waits for second alias case). Awaiting library Exchange 5/6 reply on stable-tag timeline + 4-gate handoff status (non-blocking; unlocks F+ when closed). D2 flash card scaffolding still awaits content + tech decisions. /watch/ R2 thumb caching (low-priority).

### Session K15 (2026-05-14 micro)

**K15 (2026-05-14 micro):** K14 lessons addendum (vii)+(viii) + drift restore + recovery handoff. ### Session K21 second-addendum (2026-05-15 micro)

**K21 second-addendum (same-session, post-mid-session-close):** Josiah relayed K21-commit `c2a0507` Exchange 5 ratification to book-Claude; book-Claude responded chat-side with concession + 4 trigger conditions. Two file-round-trip attempts both failed: Upload #1 byte-identical no-op (book-Claude saved nothing); Upload #2 **K4 OneDrive null-byte corruption pattern recurring** — clean 728-line state + ~1694 trailing null bytes (`^@^@^@...`) padding to 72509 bytes. Concurrently, on-disk `docs/book-claude-coordination.md` was silently mutated by sync-race mechanism to contain a TRUNCATED-MID-SENTENCE longer formal response from book-Claude (different content from both upload AND screenshot; ends "...argues against i"). Restored on-disk from HEAD via `git show HEAD:$f > $f` bypass (K12 drift-restore pattern re-validated 7th time across K9/K10/K12/K13/K15/K16/K18/K21) to clean 728-line K21 commit state; transcribed Exchange 6 from screenshot (faithful chat-summary record) as final relay artifact. **Exchange 6 content:** book-Claude conceded option-(a) Latin primary without hedging ("Anfractuous Aporia precedent argument is genuinely better than my F1 reasoning"); no flip-request from book-side; discoverability-data-driven flip door stays open. **4 book-side trigger conditions explicitly named** for next round: (i) Lacero medium decision, (ii) audio adaptation artifacts surfacing for hosting, (iii) canonical-shift flag (structural change to print canon), (iv) chat-side authorship requests for remaining Mementos / chapter-excerpts. Bilateral relay-close with explicit "nothing should cross between projects in this channel until triggers fire." Union of trigger conditions across both sides = 6 explicit conditions (book's 4 + Cowork Exchange 5's additional 2 not in book's set: new term-overload/alias case requiring book-Claude provenance; discoverability-data-driven flip request). Either side's trigger can reopen the relay. Post-Exchange-6 `docs/book-claude-coordination.md`: 746 lines / 72,677 bytes / md5 `7ff728f6ac5a2476145ff5a4c7c9e7db`. **Second-addendum lessons logged:** (xi) **K4 OneDrive null-byte corruption pattern is RECURRING vector** — joins vmwp.exe revert + `.git/index.lock` recurrence + `.git/config` truncation as ongoing failure-mode set. Upload pathway through OneDrive sync indexer can corrupt files via null-byte padding when sync races a write. Discipline: ALWAYS check upload bytes via `cat -A | tail` for null-byte tail BEFORE trusting md5/wc match; md5 match alone is insufficient when both versions corrupt to same byte length by coincidence. (xii) **Cross-Claude file relay through screenshot is canonical when file round-trip corrupts** — chat-side screenshot text is the bookmark when both endpoints (file + upload) can corrupt. Book-Claude's session-side appended response was probably valid in their session; the corruption happened in transit (download from book-Claude session → upload to Cowork). Transcription from chat capture is durable. (xiii) **Coincidence of byte-count match between two different corruption states is real-world** — upload (clean + null padding = 72509 B) and on-disk (clean + truncated content = 72509 B) hit same total by accident. `diff` flagged "Binary files differ" but `wc -lc` showed same line counts because both files ended without trailing newline at same byte position. Discipline: when file mtime + byte count look matching but content audit needed, use `cat -A | tail` to detect null-byte tails + `diff` (which uses content-comparison) to detect substantive differences. md5 catches most cases; `diff` catches the rest.

All 27 sliders byte-identical injection; 0/27 NUL/CR corruption (integrity audit confirmed). **FOUM caveat** (flash-of-unstyled-magnification): JS reads localStorage post-DOMContentLoaded so page briefly renders at default scale 1 then snaps to user's preferred size. Both files post-clean: 0 NUL / 0 CR / `</html>` close present. (4) **A Life Inside unused audio-import cleanup (micro)** — `/essays/a-life-inside/index.html` has zero `.audio-block` elements; removed 3 dead imports via Python str.replace: `<link rel="stylesheet" href="/components/audio-player.css">` + `data-audio-base="https://audio.wuld.ink"` body attr + `<script src="/components/audio-player.js"></script>`. -157B (24298 → 24141B); 0 audio refs remaining post-clean; trivially re-addable if audio is wanted later (replace `<body>` with `<body data-audio-base="...">` + re-add the 2 import lines). Note: a-life-inside also got slider markup injection from workstream 2 (essay-with-toggle inclusion). (5) **K24c narrative + memory + MEMORY.md updates + commit handoff**. Tool budget retrospective: Projected 40-55 calls (track a Tier 2); actual ~?? at close (post-commit). AskUserQuestion at session open locked track + HC approach in 2 questions per K24b lesson xii pattern; saved exploration calls on token-recolor work that wouldn't have addressed root cause. All Python writes via bash heredoc per K22 lesson vii + K24b lesson xv discipline (file-tool Edit/Write avoided on session-touched paths; 33 modified files all clean); 0 NUL bytes across all modified files; ends-with-`</html>` verified on touched HTMLs. **`<p>` margin-inline:auto audit:** N/A this turn (no vessel content centering work; slider markup is inline-flex chrome row sibling of mode-toggle). **K24c lessons logged:** (xvi) **Bulk markup injection via regex-anchor + Python slice scales cleanly to N=27 with single byte-identical block signature.** Pattern: identify byte-uniform anchor block via `re.search` + `count == 1` per file + `data[:m.end()] + injection + data[m.end():]` slice + atomic `open(path, "wb")` write + post-write audit (NUL/CR/close-tag). Reusable for any future "inject sibling component after existing component" operation. K24c achieved 27/27 clean injection in ~3 bash calls (1 audit + 1 inject + 1 verify). (xvii) **HC mode distinction is a stroke-weight problem not a color problem when color tokens are already at AAA extremes.** Pattern: when an accessibility-mode cascade only varies colors but inherits stroke/weight/spacing tokens from `:root`, the visual delta is bounded by what color can do — and at AAA extremes (`#000`/`#fff`/lifted accent/yellow focus) color can't do much beyond what's already on the page. Escalation paths from there in priority order: (a) border-width tokens — most impact, propagates to chrome separators globally; (b) font-weight tokens — depends on font-family weight availability (EB Garamond 400→600 gap, no 500 weight loaded); (c) spacing tokens — risky, can reflow layout; (d) outline-offset — narrow visibility win on focus only. K24c chose (a) alone; (b)-(d) reserved if Josiah still finds HC indistinct on second look. (xviii) **`mode-toggle.{css,js}` is now a composite chrome instrument** (mode-toggle + mag-slider sharing same files + same IIFE-friendly module shape). Decision tree for future chrome instruments (e.g., line-height slider, font-family override, color-blind palette picker): (1) shared visual register + render-adjacency with existing instruments → append to `mode-toggle.{css,js}`; (2) independent visual register OR different render-zone → new component files. Threshold judgment per-instrument; promote-to-`/components/chrome.css` if 3+ chrome-instrument components share same files. (xix) **HC verify-first approach paid off** — AskUserQuestion option `Verify toggle first, then escalate` triggered reading mode-toggle.js + cross-referencing token values BEFORE recoloring. Surface read confirmed toggle worked + colors already at extremes → escalation in correct direction (strokes not colors). Had we picked `Full rebuild assuming colors-are-close`, would have shipped a recolor that wouldn't have moved the needle + cost ~15 extra calls of mis-direction. Pattern: when user describes mode as "reads too close" to another mode, FIRST verify the toggle mechanism actually fires + SECOND audit which tokens vary vs which inherit — escalation target follows from where the inheritance gap is, not from where the visual closeness reads.

Tool budget retrospective: Projected 100-140 calls; actual ~?? at close. 2-question AskUserQuestion at session open locked track + publication path (K24b lesson xii pattern at N=3 validated). 4 mid-session operator-side breaks (PS script execution / GitHub web UI / Cloudflare Pages create / custom domain attach). All resumed with single-bash-call verification after each. **`<p>` margin-inline:auto audit:** N/A. **K24e lessons logged:** (xxiv) **PS `Set-Content -Encoding UTF8 -NoNewline` emits a BOM**. The `-NoNewline` flag controls trailing newline only; the `UTF8` encoding (in PS 5.x; renamed `UTF8NoBOM` in PS 6+) always emits the 3-byte BOM (`EF BB BF`). Pages `_redirects` parser silently rejected the BOM-prefixed rule. Workaround: `[System.IO.File]::WriteAllBytes($path, [System.Text.Encoding]::ASCII.GetBytes($content))` for pure-ASCII content (bulletproof). For UTF-8-required content, `[System.IO.File]::WriteAllText($path, $content, [System.Text.UTF8Encoding]::new($false))` is K15-canonical but verify BOM via xxd post-write. Lock: any file destined for parsers that reject BOM gets xxd-verification post-write before push. (xxv) **Cloudflare Pages "Pretty URLs" interacts with `_redirects` 200-rewrites by extension-stripping the target**: rule `/  /combined.html  200` rewrites `/` to `/combined.html` internally, then Pretty URLs 308s `/combined.html` → `/combined` externally, producing a visible redirect chain. Fix: target the extension-stripped form `/combined` directly. The `.html` form is INVALID as a rewrite target on a Pages project with Pretty URLs enabled. (xxvi) **`gh` CLI absent in default PS environment**; publication script has gh-fallback that prints description string for manual paste. Operator-side install (winget/scoop/chocolatey) would automate the description-update path but is non-blocking. (xxvii) **PS script step 11 identity-set failure mode**: freshly-cloned repo has no local `user.email`/`user.name`; global config is unset; commit refuses with "Author identity unknown". Future revision of `publish-library-*.ps1` should set local identity post-clone (between step 5 and 6): `git -C $REPO_LOCAL config user.email $WULDINK_EMAIL; git -C $REPO_LOCAL config user.name $WULDINK_NAME` with constants at script top. Carry-forward to K24f. (xxviii) **Cloudflare Workers vs Pages create-flow ambiguity**: in the merged Workers-and-Pages dashboard, the default "Connect to Git" flow creates a Workers project. The "Pages" tab is rendered in tiny secondary text (per operator feedback) and easy to miss. Workers projects require wrangler.toml or fail with `Could not detect a directory containing static files`. Lock for future similar work: explicitly verify the project type tab BEFORE clicking through. (xxix) **Pages root URL fallback behavior**: Pages serves `index.html` at `/` by default; if absent, returns 404. `_redirects` 200-rewrite is the correct fix for single-file repos where the filename is md5-binding (preserves canonical filename + serves at root); `index.html` shim or `combined.html` rename are inferior (filename-collision or filename-divergence). (xxx) **Deploy-critical chain has natural operator-side break points** (PS script execution, GitHub web UI for description, Cloudflare Pages create, Cloudflare custom domain attach). Cowork pattern at each break: emit instructions precisely + accept report-back + run single-bash-call verification before continuing. Locks for any future infra-provisioning workstream spanning operator-side dashboard work.
