JS probe via `window.innerWidth` is the reliable measurement; substrate-side `@media` enumeration + computed-style measurements at desktop viewport is the durable mobile-audit pattern. True device emulation requires DevTools Protocol, which Chrome MCP does not expose. Lock: any mobile-rendering audit goes substrate-CSS-side, not viewport-driven. (xxxvi) **K24a lesson viii sandbox-read TRUNCATION recurs after multi-tool same-file editing** — disclaimers/index.html got an Edit (§07 swap) followed by Python str.replace on the same file later. The Edit landed on Windows correctly; subsequent Python `open(path,"rb").read()` returned a TRUNCATED view of the post-Edit file (201L/13065B vs actual 219L/13674B post-Edit); Python write propagated truncation. Pattern: file-tool Edit followed by sandbox-bash read on the same file in the same session has a non-zero truncation risk. Mitigation per K24a lesson viii: derive write content from `git show HEAD:path` for any file already touched this session via Edit/Write; re-apply ALL session edits in one atomic write from the HEAD baseline. Per-file byte-delta audit (lesson ix) catches missed truncations. (xxxvii) **OG metadata wave-edit pattern is reusable for any per-page-derived bulk meta injection** (e.g., schema.org JSON-LD, RSS link refs, additional twitter:* tags). Pattern: regex-anchor on a byte-stable line (here `<meta name="description"`) + parse existing title + description as derivation source + path-to-URL canonical computation + per-page-type classification + atomic bytes write with NUL/CR/endsWith integrity audit. Idempotency via `b'property="og:title"' in data` check before injection. (xxxviii) **cairosvg pip-install pattern is durable for SVG→PNG rasterization within sandbox**: `pip install cairosvg --break-system-packages --quiet` + `cairosvg.svg2png(bytestring=..., write_to=..., output_width=..., output_height=...)`. Native viewBox respected for output dimensions; ~25KB typical output for 1200x630 simple-vector content. Reusable for any future raster-fallback need.

CSS 6738B: fixed-position bottom bar (`position: fixed; bottom: 0; height: 2.5rem; z-index: 100`), `body { padding-bottom: 2.5rem }` prevents scroll-end content overlap, hidden iframe positioned at `top: -9999px` with `width: 1px; height: 1px; opacity: 0; pointer-events: none` (off-screen rather than `display: none` so YT IFrame API can still mount + control audio), bracketed-lowercase mono button register matching mode-toggle idiom (`[play]` / `[skip]` / `[shuffle on]` / `[ambient on]`), brutalist range slider for volume (stripped `appearance: none` + `--bw-thick` track + 0.6rem x 0.9rem accent thumb), `.ambient-needs-tap` pulse animation (1.4s ease-in-out infinite opacity 1->0.45->1) on play button when autoplay denied, reduced-motion + reader-mode + HC-mode scoped overrides, 480px mobile breakpoint tightens gap + collapses volume slider to 3rem + tightens track-name max-width to 8rem. JS 12001B: single IIFE with `"use strict"` following established `mode-toggle.js` idiom. `STORAGE_KEY = "wuld:ambient"`; `DEFAULT_STATE = {on: true, volume: 40, currentVideoId: null, lastPositionSec: 0, shuffleOn: true}`. `loadYouTubeAPI()` async-injects `https://www.youtube.com/iframe_api` (which then calls global `window.onYouTubeIframeAPIReady` -> `createPlayer()`). `createPlayer()` constructs `new YT.Player("ambient-iframe", {host: "https://www.youtube-nocookie.com", playerVars: {listType: "playlist", list: PLAYLIST_ID, autoplay: state.on ? 1 : 0, controls: 0, enablejsapi: 1, modestbranding: 1, playsinline: 1, rel: 0, iv_load_policy: 3, fs: 0, origin: window.location.origin}})`. `onPlayerReady` sets volume + shuffle + defers `resumeFromSavedState()` 600ms (waits for playlist load) which uses `player.getPlaylist().indexOf(state.currentVideoId)` + `playVideoAt(idx)` + 800ms delay before `seekTo(lastPositionSec)`. `attemptInitialPlay()` calls `playVideo()` then checks player state 1400ms later; if not PLAYING/BUFFERING (autoplay denied), calls `bindFirstInteraction()` + `showNeedsTap(true)`. First-interaction listener uses `addEventListener(e, handler, true)` capture-phase on click/touchstart/keydown; one-shot via `removeEventListener` from inside handler. `STATE_SAVE_MS = 4000` periodic save covers tab-close-without-beforeunload (mobile background-kill); `beforeunload` + `visibilitychange-hidden` also save. Public surface `window.WuldAmbient = {toggle, setVolume, skip, shuffleToggle, getState}`. Track name pulled from `player.getVideoData().title`. `onPlayerError` skips forward via `nextVideo()` (region-locked or removed videos). (2) **Bulk site-wide injection N=6 of K24c lesson xvi pattern** across 45 HTML surfaces via Python regex anchor + atomic bytes write. Hit K24j lesson li adjacent failure mode: regex `image/svg+xml` initially unescaped `+` matched zero files; corrected to `image/svg\\+xml` + re-ran clean; ~1 call overhead. 5 explicit skips: `_/successor-protocol/` (sealed surface noindex,nofollow) + `glossary/black-box-of-inaccessibility/` (redirect stub) + `404.html` (error) + `templates/essay.html` + `glossary/_template.html` (templates). Post-write integrity audit 45/45 clean (0 NUL / 0 CR / `</html>` close present / `id="ambient-player"` present / both CSS + JS imports present) + 5/5 skips clean (no chrome injection). Variant indent handling: 44 files at 2-space favicon indent + 1 file (`void-engine/index.html`) at 0-space indent both handled by `[ \\t]*` capture group. (3) **Disclaimers Sec.07 YouTube transparency note** appended per honest no-tracking-ethos reconciliation. K24g lesson xxxvi mitigation: since bulk-inject in (2) already touched `src/disclaimers/index.html`, derived next-edit content from `git show HEAD:src/disclaimers/index.html` + re-applied BOTH the bulk-inject edits AND the new yt-paragraph edit in one atomic write (single subprocess + Python str.replace pipeline; sandbox-read truncation vector neutralized). New paragraph inserted before `</section>` close of Sec.07, after the Ne Hoc Fiat clause: discloses youtube-nocookie.com embed, notes Google still receives video-delivery requests when active, points readers to off-toggle escape hatch persisting across sessions. Disclaimers size 15317B (HEAD) -> 16967B (+1650B = chrome injection ~700B + yt-paragraph ~950B). Section count preserved (7); `<p>` count 24 -> 25 (one new). (4) **K24j narrative + commit handoff** - this workstream. Tool budget retrospective: Projected 80-130 (medium-heavy); actual converging well under envelope (~35-45 calls projected at commit). No subagent delegation needed (workload comfortably in main-context range). **`<p>` margin-inline:auto audit:** N/A (no centering work; ambient bar is flex layout with `<span>` track name not `<p>` element; new yt-paragraph in disclaimers uses default left-aligned `.disclaimer-section` cascade). **K24j lessons logged:** (li) **Regex `+` literal vs special-char trap** - inside a regex pattern, `+` means "one or more of preceding element"; to match a literal `+` you must escape as `\\+`. K24j hit this on `image/svg+xml` favicon anchor (matched zero files first pass). Diagnostic-test-the-regex pattern (extract anchor line + `print(f"P match: {m}")`) caught it in 1 bash call. Lock pattern: when regex matches zero files unexpectedly, FIRST test the regex against a known-positive sample bytewise BEFORE adjusting the rest of the script. (lii) **K24g lesson xxxvi pre-emptive mitigation works cleanly** - since K24j bulk-inject touched disclaimers (workstream 2), the Sec.07 edit (workstream 3) was authored as a `git show HEAD:path | python str.replace + bulk-inject re-application + atomic write` pipeline in one bash call. Zero sandbox-read truncation risk; zero phantom-state risk. Pattern: when a workstream modifies a file AND a later workstream also needs to modify the same file, derive write content from HEAD once + apply all edits in one atomic write. (liii) **User-explicit-recommendation-acceptance skips AskUserQuestion** - K24j prompt closed with "I am going with your recommended path and will be back"; this is an explicit pre-commit to track (a). AskUserQuestion at session open would have added zero information + cost 1 call. Pattern: when user message explicitly accepts a recommended track or path, skip AskUserQuestion entirely + proceed with diagnostic + execution. K24f lesson xxxi pattern (question count scales with unresolved decision axes after diagnostic) reaches its limit case at 0 questions when the user has already pre-resolved all axes. (liv) **YouTube IFrame API `setShuffle(true)` operates on YT-internal playlist order**, not externally-stable shuffle indices. Cross-page resume relies on `currentVideoId` (stable video ID) + `lastPositionSec` (stable position), NOT shuffle index (page-local). Effect: when user navigates from page A to page B, the *same video* resumes at the *same position*, but the *next track in shuffle order* may differ from what page A's shuffle would have queued next. This is acceptable for ambient register (the resume is the load-bearing UX promise; "what's next" is implicitly random anyway under shuffle). Documented in JS comments. (lv) **Existing-file content derivation from `git show HEAD:path` via `subprocess.check_output`** is the durable K24g lesson xxxvi mitigation for sandbox-read truncation. Pattern: `data = subprocess.check_output(["git", "show", f"HEAD:{path}"])` -> apply all session edits in-memory -> single atomic `open(path, "wb").write(data)`. Reusable for any multi-edit-same-file workstream pattern.

Tool budget retrospective: Projected 80–120 calls (track a end-to-end); actual ~35–45 at close. **`<p>` margin-inline:auto audit:** N/A. **K24m + K24n lessons logged:** (lxvi) **Modal-backdrop pointer-events discipline (K24m fix):** any backdrop `<div>` that contains interactive children (close button, content area) must set `pointer-events: none` on the backdrop element baseline and `pointer-events: auto` on each interactive child. Without explicit baseline, the backdrop's own click-to-close handler races with child-element handlers and the close button silently fails; Esc-only-close becomes the only reliable exit and user reads it as a stuck modal. Pattern reusable for any future overlay/modal/lightbox surface. (lxvii) **YT IFrame API playlist-mode ENDED quirk:** in `listType: "playlist"`, `YTState.ENDED` only fires at the entire playlist end, not per-video. Per-video end detection requires polling `getCurrentTime` / `getDuration` near-end window with re-fire guard (else `seekTo(0)` repeats inside the 500 ms polling window). Lock pattern for any future per-video logic over a YT playlist (per-track skip-UI, custom advance behavior, end-of-track analytics): polling > event-driven. (lxviii) **Polling-loop + drag-guard pattern for range-slider interactivity:** auto-update from polling competes with user drag; pattern = boolean flag set on `mousedown` / `touchstart` / `keydown`, cleared on window-level `mouseup` / `touchend` / `touchcancel` AND on element `blur`; polling-side updates check the flag and skip when true. Same polling loop serves multiple consumers (slider position + time readout + loop-one detection) at single setInterval cost. Reusable for any future progress-slider, scrub-bar, or auto-updating numeric control. (lxix) **`_headers` `/components/*` TTL not taking effect** — observed `max-age=14400` (4 hr) post-K24l ship where K24l intended 300 s. Possible causes: (a) Cloudflare Pages default cache-control wins over `_headers` overrides for static assets; (b) `_headers` parser silently rejected the rule; (c) edge holds the pre-`_headers` TTL. Cache-bust `?v=K24n` ritual mitigates regardless — query-string forces fresh URL. K24o diagnostic path: check Pages build log for `_headers` parser errors + try moving the rule to a more specific pattern (`/components/ambient-player.js`) to see if it's a wildcard-handling issue. Non-blocking; deploy ritual handles the immediate concern.

K24n handoff mis-read `buckets/wuld-audio?prefix=archive%2F` as "bucket=archive". K24o diagnostic-first opening caught the error in 1 bash call by direct curl-probing `https://audio.wuld.ink/archive/Hatred.pdf` which returned 200. Lock pattern: when copying dashboard URLs into infrastructure assertions, parse the path AND query params separately; if uncertain, curl the inferred resource URL directly before committing to a finding. (lxxi) **`_headers` `/components/*` SILENTLY REJECTED while other wildcards in same file work** — 8-test probe sequence confirms `_headers` parser is partial-functional: `/assets/og-default.png` + `/assets/og-default.svg` MISS-fetches return their `_headers`-specified `max-age=2592000, immutable` cleanly, but `/components/*` MISS-fetches return `max-age=14400` (Pages origin serves wrong value, not edge-cache stale). Root cause unknown; not the wildcard syntax itself (since `/assets/*` works in same file). Possible: (i) Pages parser sensitive to comment-block immediately preceding `/components/*` pathspec; (ii) parser rejects pathspec when preceding rule's last header is `Cache-Control` (continuation-parsing edge case); (iii) Pages has hardcoded override for nested-directory JS/CSS files. K24l lxv cache-bust ritual mitigates regardless. K24p experiment plan: ship `/components/ambient-player.js` exact-path rule with `max-age=600` (distinct value), probe MISS-fetch — if 600 then wildcard-only issue, if 14400 then rule-block rejected entirely. (lxxiii) **K24d lesson xx fires when audit code uses backslash-escaped byte literals inside f-strings.** Same f-string-parse-time error class as K24d. K24o hit it twice in audit-emit Python scripts — both aborted at parse before any runtime execution, so the preceding atomic-write call ALSO never ran (a script with a SyntaxError anywhere does not execute any part of itself). Workaround: precompute counts as named variables BEFORE the f-string. K24o adds: when an atomic-write call is followed by an audit-emit block in the same script, audit-block syntax errors silently abort the write. Lock pattern hardens K22 vii: keep audit logic simple (regular `print("NUL:", nul_count)` style), avoid f-string complexity in audit blocks that share a script with write calls.

AskUserQuestion 2-question shape (K24b xii pattern N=8) caught hybrid-path ambiguity in user's framing; saved ~15-20 calls of mis-execution (would have shipped unilateral override or full hold without Exchange 12 honesty). **`<p>` margin-inline:auto audit:** N/A (no centering work; new link blocks use inline anchor + span; new pointer.css consolidates existing rules byte-exact). **K24q lessons logged:** (lxxix) **Author-override-of-prior-coord-lock is a new event class for the umbrella's coord-doc family.** First instance K24q (FtP HOLD-AT-4 revision via Josiah hybrid election against Exchange 10 + Exchange 11 verdicts). Discipline pattern: (1) surface conflict at decision boundary via AskUserQuestion at session-open per K24p lxxiv; (2) ship author's elected shape cleanly without waiting for coord-Claude verdict (author authority is final, coord-doc consensus is advisory); (3) file the override in the coord-doc immediately as a new Exchange (not retcon prior Exchanges) with three response paths for the coord-Claude (lock revision / adjustments / objection); (4) await coord-Claude response next session, do NOT unilaterally re-revise pending verdict. Pattern locks for any future author-override event: library-Claude / book-Claude / successor-Claude all get treated symmetrically. (lxxx) **CSS promote-at-N=3-with-non-shared-CSS is hygiene, not duplication-elimination.** When the N=3 classes share semantic role (idiom) but have meaningfully different visual rules (different sizing, different chrome, different cascade attachments), promoting to a shared component file is file-shuffle hygiene - single-source-of-truth for any future N=4+ pointer + cross-component cache key - but does NOT reduce CSS bytes or improve cascade. Acceptable when bounded cost + clear future expansion expectation; prefer N=4+ with actual CSS-duplication for true promote ROI. Lock pattern: at any N=3 promote decision, honestly assess (a) is the CSS actually duplicated? if yes, promote with base-class extraction; (b) if no, promote-as-idiom-consolidation only when bounded cost + future expansion likely; (c) if no on both, defer to N=4+. K24q chose (b) at bounded ~30-50 calls actual ~25 calls; pointer.css ships with header-comment documenting the idiom + naming convention for K25+. (lxxxi) **AskUserQuestion options should include hybrid paths when user framing suggests one.** K24q AskUserQuestion offered 3 paths on FtP (hold / reopen via coord-doc / unilateral override); Josiah's actual answer was a 4th hybrid path (4 anchors stay + link exists). Cowork pattern improvement: when crafting AskUserQuestion options on a decision with potential hybrid resolutions, include the hybrid as an explicit option rather than relying on user's "Other" text - explicit hybrid option signals to user that Cowork has considered it + avoids the option-frame anchoring user toward extreme answers. K24q deferred hybrid recognition until user supplied it; pattern next session: pre-anticipate hybrid + include explicitly. (lxxxii) **Multi-edit Python atomic-write pattern N=5 validated** (K24q /archive/ shipped 4 successive byte-exact str.replace in single Python script + post-write JSON-LD parse validation): first pass anchor-miss recovery via re-derive from HEAD + corrected anchors + single-script second-pass. Lock pattern: when planning multi-edit on a single file, draft all anchors + replacements in one Python script with per-step `data.count(anchor) == 1` audit; if any anchor misses, fix the script (not the disk) + re-run from HEAD. NEVER pile edits across multiple Python scripts on same disk file (compounds K24a viii sandbox-read truncation vector + leaves intermediate states on disk).
